Call them tainted and they'll laugh at you. Call them worthless and they’ll ignore you. Call them dogs and they'll leave you bleeding on the asphalt. The Bone Gnawers have been fighting to survive in the harsh réalm 6f the'city for millennia, and they’re just about finished taking crap from everyone else. The lowest of Garou are ready to prove that social standing isn’t everything — to survive on the streets of the World of Darknéss, you need teeth. . ; Every Woffttas His; Day sg The most dangerous of the urban werewolves get their due in the new Tribebook: Bone Gnawers. Inside you'll find the tricks of survival that have’ kept the Gnawers around for so long, as well ‘as the nuances of their downand-out society. Tribebook: Bone Gnawers contains more than twice“as much information as the original — expanded history, current events, social conventions, hidden traditions, plenty of new Gifts, rites, fetishes and other rules, hints of things to Come, and even more. .
